< Review>
Terrible food, service, everything. Me and my girlfriend ordered here because we thought it'd be like tapioca express. Super wrong, I ordered the asada fries cause I haven't had anything like that in while and my girlfriend ordered a chicken combo w/ passion fruit slush. The chicken combo was super bland and dry, and didnt remotely taste anything of east asian cuisine. The asada fries we thought were better, but after awhile we got upset stomachs.  The passion fruit slush had chunks of ice and after drinking it awhile was just watered down chunks of ice with no flavor. We didnt even finish our food or drink due to how bad they were. Super slow service as well.

Never ever coming here again.

Side note - while we were waiting for our food, a homeless man came in with no mask. He then puts on his mask already standing in the restaurant, and walks around. He then receives a boba milk tea without prior interaction with the cashier and leaves. It's great if you want to help the homeless in these times, but putting your other customers at risk during a pandemic should not be a priority over customers already in the store waiting for their order.

If you're looking at this page and reading this review, go to Tapioca Express instead. The food and drinks are 1000% better then this place.

Would give 0 stars if it was possible.< /Review>

< review>
Cool vibe. Chill music. Very friendly staff. They ran out of the bread for my sandwich that I had ordered for take out. When I got in they were very apologetic and offered a couple of upgrades for free.

Very Island feel inside. The food is fabulous. They have beer and great cold sandwiches and hot sandwiches.

Giving it four stars instead of 5 because this isn't the first time they have run out of something that we wanted to order. They get very busy and doesn't seem like they stock enough.</review>

<review>Despite the cashier being a bit slow and not willing to take a proper order, I think this place is one of the best pizza places in the valley!

This franchised Ameci's location in Granada Hills has the friendliest owner. The specials are usually good enough prices for a family to save on a delicious dinner. So here's my experience today. I went into order something for lunch on a Friday afternoon. It was about 4:00 p.m. I approached the cashier and asked her what lunch specials they had or personal sized pizzas that were available.

The cashier immediately said no we don't offer that even though there was clearly a personal size pan pizza box taped up to the wall to show the special.  I asked her again and she proceeded to say no until the manager said what are you talking about get this guy a couple slices. He asked how many I wanted, and I said 2 pepperoni.

I asked for a can soda as well. The total was about $4. Within 2 minutes and I was served four slices of pepperoni pizza and a can of coke. The people is amazing. Fresh, cooked to perfection just the right amount of toppings and overall I can say that I was completely satisfied.

This place is always a good choice for lunch or dinner. I'm definitely coming here again.<//review></record></dataset><record>

Henry Jr. informed us that his dad would come in early and stay late to get our work done and get us back on the road by Friday. <rate>5< /rate>< Text>
Integrity Transmission was truly a God send to me last year. Not only did they install a transmission for **HALF** the price I was quoted at the dealer, but what is worth every penny is how efficient and professional they are with everything.

My transmission blew while I was on the 405 freeway, and Honda wanted $$$$ to replace it, practically a down payment for a new car! After considering my options and even going through the sales process for a new vehicle, I took to Yelp and requested ~20 quotes from shops near Carson (where the car broke down) and not only did Integrity come up with the best offer, but every part of the process was so quick, painless and exceeded ALL of my expectations:

- Henry called me in less than an hour with a quote, based on the diagnosis I described by Honda
- He had an estimate e-mailed to me quickly so I could authorize the repair
- He had my car towed from Honda to their shop for a small cost, and I was able to authorize that via DocuSign instead of having to leave work to be present
- Most correspondence was done by text, which is so much more simple and effective than playing phone tag!
- Everything done was so transparent, from photos and videos of the transmission damage, to photos of readings they did to test the car and support their recommendations, to photos of the new transmission and installation (all of this communicated by text)
- They outline everything in revised repair orders sent via e-mail to ensure you authorize it and are on the same page
- All paperwork was done online via DocuSign - I never had to leave work to go to their shop or do anything. The one and only time I went to the shop was to pick up my car!

To show you how quickly they work: (closed weekends)
- the car got towed to them late Thursday 3/8,
- they diagnosed the car on Friday 3/9,
- my new transmission was delivered to them on Monday 3/12,
- I had the car back by early afternoon on Tuesday 3/13

On top of that, they offered to deliver my finished car to me for free as part of the service. I declined since I had to return my rental car close to them anyway, but how awesome is it that you could have a completely remote auto repair experience??

I am truly still in shock about this experience, how easy and painless they made everything, and how happy I am about the repairs made to the car. The car feels brand new and drives as if nothing ever happened - stark difference from when it slowly died on me on the freeway, breathing its last breath of life, LOL. If you have ever had to deal with a major auto repair before, you know how painful and prolonged it can be. I am so grateful to Integrity Transmission for completely turning this experience around!

Thank you, Henry and team, SO much for this experience! I cannot say enough good things or thank you enough for saving my car, making this as painless as possible for me, and being so transparent and upfront with how you run your business! Everyone needs to come here!</Text>

I work close by so I'm thankful that they opened up a AT&T store around the corner. I've been in there at least 5x now and 4/5 times that I've been in there the customer service was excellent!
My first time in there Jorge was the one who helped me out (too bad he got transferred) with my dads replacement phone. He called customer service (I think) and had them activate my fathers phone- but they messed up and switched my phone with his phone.. Overall it was super messy and confusing , but Jorge fixed it without breaking a sweat! :)
(He told me to take their survey to rate them but I never received the survey)

Second experience, I had one day left to pay for my phone bill, usually I would mail a check but that would take at least a couple of days to process so I decided to walk in and pay instead. Their rules were they did not accept more than $600 in cash but they very helpful and nice and let me slide this one time. :) (another good experience, sad though I didn't catch her name but she was a Latina woman; so helpful in explaining why I'm getting charge for random as stuff)

Third experience, phone bill again and had to buy phone case and screen protector for dad. I should seriously get the names of the employees that helped me out... This guy was super chill and honest and made it very easy to communicate with. I usually don't like dealing with AT&T employees cause they're only there to steal/take your money. But this guy (he has a pizza tattoo) was very helpful and throughly explained a lot about my bill and phone contract for me!

Fourth experience, I was being to hopeful thinking that I would never have a problem with this AT&T store.. Walked in there with the same problem to help my "brother" activate his replacement phone. It wasn't busy at all in fact I was the only customer in there. I had two issues; activate my brothers phone and hoping to switch my name to the account holder (if you haven't noticed I'm the one who always have to deal with my family's phone situations) anyways, the blonde lady (the manager) asked me what the problem was. I told her I needed to activate my brothers phone. I didn't think there would be a problem since I activated my dads phone before without my mom being there (mom is the account holder). She asked me for my ID to make sure my name was under the account and next thing I knew she handed me back my phone and said she can't do anything if the account holder isn't here. What?! She told me to call customer service myself and tell them to change the icic because the SIM card was not activated or the right one? Like what?! Care to explain? She didn't seem to care and she seemed annoyed and didn't want to bother helping me at all. So I just left. Smh (Even though this was the worst experience yet, I'm still going to give them 5/5 stars because all the other employees were so helpful.)

So the next day I returned again with my mom this time. And the guy with the pizza tattoo (I wished I remembered his name) helped us out! Activated my brothers phone within seconds and I was done! How quick and easy was that? I asked him about he account holder situation and he explained that this store is only limited to doing certain things and another employee suggested that we go to the main store in San Leandro. And this is why I still gave them 5/5 stars because majority of their employees are super nice, friendly and very helpful!

I wish I recieved the survey so I can take it and review you guys! Your store has been super helpful and is so convienent since I'm just around the corner! Keep up the good work you guys! :D< /review>

< text>
I was about to sell my old car, which had 93,000 miles on it, when I received a lemon-law mailer from Goldsmith. Although the car was in great shape and running fine, I had the transmission replaced twice at 70,000 miles and 76,000 miles. But the manufacturer had replaced both transmissions free and even paid for my rental car while mine was in the shop. And this was all done well after the 60,000-mile drive-train warranty had expired.

I thought my chances of getting any settlement money were dim. On a lark, I called David and asked him a lot of questions. He assured me I had a strong case and that I would never have any legal bills regardless of the outcome. His confidence in the case convinced me to give it a shot.

He expected a settlement in three to fourth months. In reality, it ended up taking around six months before the manufacturer bought the car back and I was paid. That was the only slightly negative experience about the whole process. Whenever I checked in for a progress report, David or his assistant Kaitlyn would return my call the same day. One time, he even called from Joshua Tree National Park where he was on a camping trip.

The bottom line: The settlement from the manufacturer was $10,000 more than I would have received by selling to a private party. And on top of that, the manufacturer separately paid all my legal costs.

I highly recommend this firm.<//text>

< Review>
The coffee and tea here is great, the staff is friendly and helpful. I‚Äôve tried a variety of drinks here and they were all delicious and well-made. There‚Äôs nothing like a vanilla tea latte to relax or a cafe Cubano to wake up. I like the pastries especially the tres leches muffin which they very kindly offer to heat up for you. Even during these trying times, the staff manage to create a welcome atmosphere while keeping customers safe through social distancing, wearing masks, and even offering sanitizer. I would recommend this place to everybody that loves coffee and amazing staff!< /Review>

< Review>
We were staying next door at the Best Western for a few days and stopped by here each morning.
The
Place was clean and inviting, and had that fresh brewed coffee smell as soon as we entered.

< Review>
We were staying next door at the Best Western for a few days and stopped by here each morning.
The
Place was clean and inviting, and had that fresh brewed coffee smell as soon as we entered.
It does have a very familiar layout if you visit other chain coffee shops, pastry display case next to where you order, with The barista next to that.
Very familiar & comfortable.
The staff while we were there were amazing!
Very friendly and helpful.
We only had the brewed coffee, but it was very good. Not bitter at all, plenty of flavor.
I also had to try, (and try the next day also üòú), the Tres Leche Muffin... very good!!
I can‚Äôt speak for all the locations, but this one is a must if you need coffee in the area<//Review>

< review>
I don't like coffee nor am a "caffeine junkie."  Update: (Now I'm a coffee lover!) Occasionally, I do make the exception every so often whenever I drink a cold beverage from this Latin inspired cafe. Generally, I purchase a small Marizpan drink once or twice a month and a small pastry alongside. It's usually not too crowed during the week days but during the weekend it is. Unlike Starbucks, this cafe won't have sandwiches or bacon gourdas, so a note of precaution, don't get upset if you don't find it here. With that mind, dine in here! Fun fact: This is the first Tierra Mia Coffee from it's franchise.</review>

< username>
Aj Herrera</username>
< Text>
Excellent service, great menu. Most of the staff are always in a great mood. I've only come across one or two cashiers with a 'whatever, I don't really want to be here" attitude but the rest of the staff makes up for that.

Prices are reasonable on most items but Im still not sold on paying over four dollars for a cup of Joe. Specialty drinks?ok. Cup of coffee?.. NO.
I would expect that from some silly place like blue bottle or the classic and pretentious handsome coffee roasters.

Nice assortment of pastries (not frozen, btw. They make their own not far from here) so kuddos for that. I come here to edit on my laptop and for the white noise which Allows me to get in the zone.

I do love the fact that they do not have Wi-Fi and that is because they want to promote social interaction. It is pretty refreshing to look around and see people engaging with each other as oppose to a room full of people with their faces burried in their devices or doing that stupid vertical zombie swipe as they stare blankly into their phone.

Gets a little busy at 7pm ish and if you can drown out the occasional children running around you will be fine.

Over all I like this place. No snobbery from baristas or foul attitudes.

Henry is usually on shift when I come. I love his positive attitude He's always working hard, multi tasking, supporting his team and always goes out of his way  to acknowledge the guests.</Text>
